Matricide is probably the most unbearable crime of all ... and most unbearable to the son who commit it. So he had to erase the crime, at least in his own mind. He stole her corpse ... and a weighted coffin was buried. He hid the body in the fruit cellar, even `` treated'' it to keep it as well as it would keep. And that still wasn't enough. She was there, but she was a corpse. So he began to think and speak for her, gave her half his life, so to speak.
